flödet för att konversera genom en slutkursutvärdering
own experience " alright , first let me ask you a few questions about your personal experience " - " how many hours per week did you spend on the course , including scheduled hours ? " - &lt;10 hrs - 11-20 hrs - 21-40 hrs - &gt;40 hrs
- " did you think that there was a reasonable workload ? " - yes : next question - no : " why not ? " - of what ? : " the course in general . " - " how was the pace ? " - if good : next question - if " bad " or similar : " how do you suggest to improve it ? " - of what ? : " the course in general . " - " did the course interest you ? " - yes : " what was most interesting ? " - no : " why not ? " - " how would you describe your own effort in this course ? " / " tell me about your effort in this course . " - " in short , what have you learned ? " instructor " thanks ! i 've got some questions about the instructor too . " - " how was the instructors availability ? " - good : next question - bad : " how it be improved ? " - " did you get the help that you needed ? " - yes : next question - no : " what did you need then ? " - " how about feedback on e.g . assignments and tests , did you find that valuable ? " - yes : next question - no : " what was missing ? " - " did the instructor explain the content in a way that helped you learn ? " - yes : " what did you find most helpful ? " - no : " what would help you learn better ? " - " how did you experience the instructors enthusiasm ? " - " how would you describe your overall experience of the instructor ? " " what 's your experience of the administration of the course ? think schedule , exam signup , etc . " " were the goals , objectives and grades clearly presented to you early in the course ? " - yes : next question - no : " what was missing ? " - " did the taught material match what was presented in the syllabus ? " - yes : next question - no : " tell me what did n't match . " - " how do you think the fairness of the grading was ? " - positive : next question - negative : " what was unfair ? " " what did you think of the course material ? i mean for example literature , articles , media , etc . " - positive : " glad to hear that ! what made it good ? " - negative : " sorry to hear that , how could it improve ? " " what 's your view of the subject itself ? " " what 's your overall experience of the course ? " " tell me something that you think could be improved . " " tell me what absolutely should not be excluded from the course . " " is there something else you would like to comment on ? " - yes : " what ? " - no : " ok , thanks ! " exempel med topics och sentiment för utbrytning av förslag " hi . . etc . today i'm going to ask you about these things : - literature
- digital content
- seminars
- labs " " click one you would like to start evaluating " neutral topic ? h : " so what did you think about the course literature ? " s : " so neither good or bad ? what could improve it ? " positiv topic
h : " so what did you think about the course literature ? " s : " great " - [type : positive feedback] h : " i'm glad to hear that ! what made it so great ? " s : " the fact that it felt very up do date and was well written " - [type : feedback]
- [topic : literature]
- [reason : up to date]
- [reason : well written] negativ topic
h : " so what did you think about the course literature ? " s : " terrible " - [type : negative feedback] h : " i'm sorry to hear that ! how could it be improved ? " s : " we should have more modern books and not so much to read " - [type : feedback]
- [topic : literature]
- [suggestion : more modern books]
- [suggestion : not so much to read]

<url>

[U3PEE7BCJ]
vi gör 'intent classification' och 'entity extraction' . spacy - nlp for tokenization , dependency parsing , et.c . word2vec or glove for word embeddings as input to the ner and classification models . intent classification uses a linear svm optimized using a grid search . we use conditional random fields to do named entity recognition ( " crf ner " ) . crfs can be thought of as an undirected markov chain where the time steps are words and the states are entity classes . features of the words ( capitalisation , pos tagging , etc. ) give probabilities to certain entity classes , as are transitions between neighbouring entity tags : the most likely set of tags is then calculated and returned . we have also tried mitie as an alternative to spacy / sklearn .

huvudsyftena med svaren delas in i olika " taggar " ; ex . " start having morning lectures " och " stop having lectures late in the day " taggas som [schedule] . taggarna kategoriseras som bra eller förbättringsmöjlighet efter vad studenterna har sagt inom respektive tagg i utvärderingen . i exemplet ovan är [schedule] en förbättringsmöjlighet , då bägge svaren är förslag på förändringar . för varje huvudsyfte sparas huvudord samt beskrivningsord , ex . " morning lectures " och " having " två topplistor sammanställs : bra och förbättringsmöjligheter . en skriven sammanfattning görs av den översta taggen i respektive lista , vilket ger en mer detaljerad bild av vad som kan förbättras . i denna återfinns med konkreta tips såsom förslag på hur lektionerna ska schemaläggas enligt exemplet ovan .

[U2D5B8PLL]
lite generella problem med att säkra validitet i kursutvärderingar , för den som känner sig rastlös : 1 - the use of instructors to collect forms rating their own instructional merit . 2 - lack of controls over pleas for sympathy or indulgence by the teacher before forms are distributed . 3 - inadequate time to complete forms . 4 - failing to ensure an acceptable return rate . problem med dataprocessing , rapportdesign och tolkning
1 - the use of averages alone , without regard to the distribution;
2 - failure to set up appropriate comparison groups so that the usual tendency for ratings to be higher in graduate professional schools can be taken into account;
3 - treating small differences as significant , just because they are statistically significant;
4 - using factor analysis without logical / theoretical validation;
5 - ignoring ceiling / floor effects;
6 - using the ratings as the sole basis for either formative or summative evaluation .

- allt som är rappakalja ska bort ( vi vet inte vad som är rappakalja , ingen kan sätta fingret på det iaf ) - följdfråga - hur ska vi definiera rappakalja ? - vi bestämmer ett antal tecken som utgör en besvärlig mening , längre meningar än så ber hubert studenten att korta ner
- vi är inte rädda för att säga till både studenter och lärare att hubert ännu lär sig ( vi tar ju inte ens betalt än ) och vi måste jobba med att sätta förväntningar rätt så att ingen får mindre än de har förväntat sig
- vi ska alltid svara , alltid vara relevanta , alltid ödmjuka
- vi bortser från de 3-4% som alltid är idioter
- bo har en våt dröm om trepunktsrapporter " gör dessa tre saker så blir du bättre " , vilket jag tycker är ett bra långsiktigt mål . konkret och trevligt . - mvp innehåller bara hubert score och klickbara topplistor ( vilket är mycket bättre än vad läraren har som alternativ redan idag ) - vi ska undersöka möjligheterna att utveckla en deep learning-modell där turkar sammanfattar data till en konkret rekommendation / summering
- vi vet inte vad vi vill innan vi kan beskriva det som om en femåring skulle utföra uppgiften
- vi börjar jobba undercover med en analysmodell under tiden vi har lanserat vår mvp , förhoppningsvis trillar massor av data in

[U2D5ENN2C]
we at <url> are striving towards a better system for student evaluations of teaching and course assessments in higher education . using a chatbot to collect feedback comes with an exciting set of new possibilities and a solution to many issues that are present in sets today . our aim is to train hubert to become an expert teacher-instructor that takes in student feedback , automatically analyzes it and compiles the feedback down to a few actionable recommendations on how the teacher could improve professional skills best . as hubert grows smarter we hope to draw conclusions on what teacher methods and pedagogical approaches work best based on teacher feedback from all over the world and propose a way of implementing them directly in the course . a known way to collect more detailed opinions from respondents in both market research and student evaluations is to have qualitative interviews instead of just using survey forms . this way of collecting feedback is generally known for quality , hence the name . advantages are that you can ask follow-up questions and adapt the interviews to interesting responses or unclear statements . the downside is of course that it takes a lot of time and is expensive . with <url> you get the best from two worlds . in the future , hubert will be able to follow up on interesting opinions and customize the interview without you having to pay an expensive salary to an interview administrator . over time hubert can get to know each and every student , keep track of previously taken courses , interest , and personal preferences and can suggest other courses to the students . this way it 's also possible to tackle survey bias related to student interests . both instructors and students will save considerable amounts of time by using hubert . instructors save time , both on sending out the survey and on the analysis which is automatically completed . students' saves time on lengthy surveys , as they can answer many questions in the same sentence without even giving it an extra thought . other advantages with hubert include : -it 's more fun for students to have a conversation with a chatbot rather than filling out boring surveys ( higher response rates ) -it 's possible for students to choose which medium to communicate with hubert through . options right now include the hubert web-app , facebook messenger , slack , and email . other features that we are working on : - automatically filter out vulgar language and insults . - follow-up questions to unclear student statements
- continuous evaluations throughout the duration of the course
- lti-compliance
- hubert should be able to customize dialog with every student , i.e . learn personal stuff and follow up with questions on topics that were discussed last time .
